12 Dec 2016 08:31:14 : The Wild Weebs, general, Wertfuzzy77#0274, ```Question 5
A == 1 = Set Alarm
B == 1 = Catch 8:30 Bus
L == 1 = Late for Class

P(A = 1) = 3/4 : Probability that Alarm set
P(B = 1|A = 1) = 4/5 : Probability that you catch 8:30 Bus, given that Set Alarm
P(B = 1|A = 0) = 2/5 : Probability that catch 8:30, Given no Alarm set'
P(L = 1|B = 1) = 1/4 : Probability of Late, given Catch Bus
P(L = 1|B = 0) = 2/3 : Probability of Late, given didnt catch Bus

5.1
P(A = 0) = 1/4
P(B = 0|A = 1) = 1/5
P(B = 0|A = 0) = 3/5
P(L = 0|B = 1) = 3/4
P(L = 0|B = 0) = 1/3

5.2
[  A  ]
   |    [P(1) = 3/4]
  \ /    [P(0) = 1/4]
   '
[  B  ]
   |    [P(1) = 4/5 * 3/4 + 2/5 * 1/4 = .7] 
  \ /    [P(0) = 1/5 * 3/4 + 3/5 * 1/4 = .3] 
   '
[  L  ]
    [P(1) = 1/4 * .7 + 2/3 * .3 = .375]
    [P(0) = 3/4 * .7 + 1/3 * .3 = .625]  

5.3
P(A = 1, B = 1, L = 0) = 
= P(A = 1) * P(B = 1| A = 1) * P(L = 0|B = 1)
= 3/4 * 4/5 * 3/4 
= .45

5.4
P(B = 1)
= .7

5.5
P(L = 0)
= .625

5.6
P(L = 1,A = 0)
= .375 * .25 = .09375 

5.7
P(L = 1|A = 0)
= 3/5*2/3 + 2/5*1/4
= .5```
